<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Papa's House is a landmark in Stallion Springs. The new owners carry on the tradition of making and serving the best food possible! The menu has a little something for everyone, they also take care of those with dietary issues often times going out of their way to create something to suit your needs!  The staff is welcoming and create that small town feel where everyone is family! Great service, always with a smile even when you drop in at the end of the day and they are about to close exhausted and ready to go home to their families you become their family in that moment!  Highly recommended taking a trip out to the Springs to check it out you won't be disappointed!< /Review>

<user_name>Daniel Choi< /user_name><Time>1541277372123</Time><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
Traffic around SF has reached a breaking point, especially around Yerba Buena where I live. A buddy from my office picked up a scooter and couldn't stop talking about how it changed his mobility around the city, so I decided to look into it.

I've ridden scooters before but consider myself a newbie, so I shopped around a bit. Was looking for something with a smaller footprint that could take short highway trips and fit a second passenger comfortably. Quick piece of advice ‚Äì¬†don't go to a motorcycle shop that ALSO sells scooters. The couple places like this I checked out had a seriously limited scooter selection, far less knowledgeable salespeople, and generally chunkier rides that seemed more like riffs off Honda cycles.

Ended up at SF Scooter Centre, and knew that this was where I'd pick up my new scooter. Barry and Diego, the guys running the front desk, were attentive, knowledgeable, and generally fun dudes. Also full of practical knowledge that they offered proactively ‚Äì¬†while I was there, a woman came in to buy a helmet and her and Barry got to talking about the scooter she was planning to buy off Craigslist. Barry told her she might want to call around to scooter shops in the area and ask them if they could service the model (because no one would want to). This useful tip was offered with zero condescension and no pressure to buy something from the shop instead.

Anyway, I spent over an hour checking out the different models, learning a ton from Barry about the pros/cons. All their scooters are pretty sleek, which presented the only challenge ‚Äì picking out which model and color I wanted! Ended up coming out with a great deal on a new Buddy 170i in British racing green w/ white striping. The thing is a compliment machine, and I'm loving bombing around SF on it.

Even better, the shop also handles servicing and sells vintage scooters if that's your speed. I couldn't recommend them more highly. It's awesome to feel like you've got "a scooter guy" for all your current and future needs.

Thanks Barry and Diego!<//text>

<review>Barry Gwin, the owner of San Francisco Scooter Center (stylized - spelled "Centre") is knowledgeable and sells only the products that he believes in. Since 2004 I have bought 10 scooters from him.

Currently, he features the Genuine Buddy scooter line. They range in size from 125cc to 170cc. He also has the Buddy Kick.

In November 2018 I bought a Buddy 170i. That's the fuel injected model. I bought that to replace my 125 buddy that was stolen in October 2018. I had bought that 125 from Barry in 2007. That buddy never gave me a problem always look good  and was a great scooter.  That's why I bought another one that looks exactly the same, except it is a 2013.

Barry gave me a great price and a 60-day bumper to bumper warranty. That's excellent considering warranties nowadays that he would give me a 60-day 100% warranty.

I highly recommend that you check out Barry's store. You will not be disappointed. If anything you can tap his mind and expertise and know a lot more about scooters from when you walked in the door.

Note, he is closed on Mondays and maybe on Sundays. So if you're going to shop on the weekend make sure it's on a Saturday. San Francisco Scooter Center is on 10th, close to Mission. Plenty of scooter parking or motorcycle, and metered parking.

Warning, 10th Street is an aggressive thoroughfare for people to get around so be careful when on a scooter that you don't get mowed down by a car.<//review></record></dataset><record>

< review>
My husband usually goes to his barber but due to his schedule he wasn‚Äôt able to make an appointment with his barber, he needed to run a formal errand and decided to go to this place for a haircut. After a few days of getting his haircut here he started to get really itchy in the back of his head. I assumed it was a rash to the pillows. We changed pillows, pillow cases, different soap, stopped using hair wax and products, changed hair brushes and even shampoo, but the rash only got worse and even started getting bumps on his head. After looking online the only reasonable thing was folliculitis. A rash that is developed by lack of hygiene of tools used to cut hair or shave. Since he hasn‚Äôt gotten a haircut since then, there is no way he could of gotten this from anywhere else.
I suppose if you‚Äôre willing to live with the torture of being itchy, loose your hair or even spread to others around you... definitely go.</review>

< Review>
My family and I have driven past this place dozens of times and finally decided to give it a try today for lunch. Like other have stated the menu is small just a few breakfast choices. Some appetizers. A 4 item kids choice and a few other things.

I decided to go ahead and order some breakfast so I went with the French toast. You can get a half size or a full size. I did the half and I'm glad I did the full might have been a little too much for me. It was delicious. These French toast actually had flavor to them unlike alot of other places. My parents ordered the tacos which they said were good. And the chips and salsa that they give are yummy.

Everything is made fresh to order so don't expect your food to come out super fast.</Review>

<gmapID>0x80c336a243dcde2f:0x4bc0a829d5fccb22<//gmapID><pics>None</pics><text>I'm on the fence on whether I want to give a 3 or 4 Star review. My husband and I came here for the first time on Sunday 10/1/2017. We arrived at 8:30AM.  We pulled into the lot right after another vehicle, but they were not busy at all at this time.

Since I saw they allow dogs here (from Yelp), we had two of our dogs with us and asked to sit outside. Our server came outside after 5 minutes to give us menus and take our drink order. We did not see her again for another 10 minutes. My husband and I decided to share the Chile Verde burrito and the "Eggtastic" breakfast which included biscuits and gravy, sausage or bacon, 2 eggs, and potatoes.

The quaint outdoor area has cute decor and has plenty of seating; including picnic benches. There are games to play such as cornhole (bean bag toss), horseshoe toss, and even Jenga. There are also people riding their bikes or walking.

The Biscuits & Gravy were the first to come out. Although delicious, I thought the biscuits underneath the gravy were cold. Our server also brought a bowl of water for our dogs which was kind.

After that, the rest of our meal took about 30 minutes. We had the whole back patio/play area to ourselves so we were able to keep ourselves occupied, but may have been a different scenario if we were sitting inside and staring at the wall.

The chile verde wet burrito had good flavors, but my husband said his half only had about 2 pieces of meat in it while mine had more. It had a bit of a kick to it, but my husband said he didn't like the texture of the tortilla. He's had better wet burritos. The sausage that came with the Eggtasic plate were very tasty and the potatoes were delicious. Our bill came out to $25.00.

Overall, I give it a 3. When I discussed our overall experience with my husband we did conclude that we would return but that we shouldn't come hungry. We would probably just get an order of nachos and some tacos and relax on their back patio; knowing that the food takes a while. Our server also mentioned that they are expecting to put TVs outside.  This place has potential with its location and menu offerings so an updated review may be warranted in the future.</text>< date>

Nosotros ordenamos tajaditas con carne molida y cebolla en curtido. Tambi√©n ordenamos la especial de 6 baleadas por $1.25 cada una. Todo estuvo muy delicioso. Un poco caro por las tajaditas pero no estamos en Honduras entonces "it's worth the price" lol.

We got the plantain chips with ground beef and Honduran sauce with the pink pickled onions (super yum). We also ordered the special of the day that was 6 baleadas for $1.25 each which is a deal bc normal price one is $2.99. the tajaditas are a bit pricey if you compare to how much they cost in Honduras but since we out here in Cali it's definitely worth the price. <review>i really like this restaurant but the reason i am not giving it 5 stars is because i had a bad experience one time. It wasn't the food, but i bought a coupon on groupon for $11. This $11 coupon has a $22 worth at the restaurant. So i purchased 2 of them. The coupon said $22 because that's how much i payed. I gave that coupon to my husband as an early birthday present. We went to eat and i asked the waiter what can i get with this coupon he recommended we get the PARILLADA. So we got that with 2 drinks. The food was AMAZING. really yummy. i have no complaints about that. we got a little bit of everything on that parillada. if i remember correctly the bill came to be around $25-$30. Then he discounted $22. The coupon was suppose to discount double which is $44. I told him and he said sorry but the coupon says $22 ...you can talk to them if you have an issue. Later i found out it was my mistake and that u can only use one coupon per table. So his mistake actually gave me the real discount without his knowledge though. If the coupon said $11 he would of given me $11 instead of $22. I just think if your going to deal with groupon you should have your stuff together. Yes it was my mistake as well but he could of explained what groupon explained to me, but he had no idea the coupon was actually worth $22. Either then that the food and service is great. I recommend paying with cash or credit when you go and avoid the coupons.</review>< username>
